5939    /**
5940     * Removes the first substring of the text string that matches the given regular expression.
5941     *
5942     * This method is a {@code null} safe equivalent to:
5943     * <ul>
5944     *  <li>{@code text.replaceFirst(regex, StringUtils.EMPTY)}</li>
5945     *  <li>{@code Pattern.compile(regex).matcher(text).replaceFirst(StringUtils.EMPTY)}</li>
5946     * </ul>
5947     *
5948     * <p>A {@code null} reference passed to this method is a no-op.</p>
5949     *
5950     * <p>The {@link Pattern#DOTALL} option is NOT automatically added.
5951     * To use the DOTALL option prepend {@code "(?s)"} to the regex.
5952     * DOTALL is also known as single-line mode in Perl.</p>
5953     *
5954     * <pre>
5955     * StringUtils.removeFirst(null, *)      = null
5956     * StringUtils.removeFirst("any", (String) null)  = "any"
5957     * StringUtils.removeFirst("any", "")    = "any"
5958     * StringUtils.removeFirst("any", ".*")  = ""
5959     * StringUtils.removeFirst("any", ".+")  = ""
5960     * StringUtils.removeFirst("abc", ".?")  = "bc"
5961     * StringUtils.removeFirst("A&lt;__&gt;\n&lt;__&gt;B", "&lt;.*&gt;")      = "A\n&lt;__&gt;B"
5962     * StringUtils.removeFirst("A&lt;__&gt;\n&lt;__&gt;B", "(?s)&lt;.*&gt;")  = "AB"
5963     * StringUtils.removeFirst("ABCabc123", "[a-z]")          = "ABCbc123"
5964     * StringUtils.removeFirst("ABCabc123abc", "[a-z]+")      = "ABC123abc"
5965     * </pre>
5966     *
5967     * @param text  text to remove from, may be null
5968     * @param regex  the regular expression to which this string is to be matched
5969     * @return  the text with the first replacement processed,
5970     *              {@code null} if null String input
5971     *
5972     * @throws  java.util.regex.PatternSyntaxException
5973     *              if the regular expression's syntax is invalid
5974     *
5975     * @see #replaceFirst(String, String, String)
5976     * @see String#replaceFirst(String, String)
5977     * @see java.util.regex.Pattern
5978     * @see java.util.regex.Pattern#DOTALL
5979     * @since 3.5
5980     *
5981     * @deprecated Moved to RegExUtils.
5982     */
5983    @Deprecated
5984    public static String removeFirst(final String text, final String regex) {
5985        return replaceFirst(text, regex, EMPTY);
5986    }
5987
5988    /**
5989     * Case insensitive removal of all occurrences of a substring from within
5990     * the source string.
5991     *
5992     * <p>
5993     * A {@code null} source string will return {@code null}. An empty ("")
5994     * source string will return the empty string. A {@code null} remove string
5995     * will return the source string. An empty ("") remove string will return
5996     * the source string.
5997     * </p>
5998     *
5999     * <pre>
6000     * StringUtils.removeIgnoreCase(null, *)        = null
6001     * StringUtils.removeIgnoreCase("", *)          = ""
6002     * StringUtils.removeIgnoreCase(*, null)        = *
6003     * StringUtils.removeIgnoreCase(*, "")          = *
6004     * StringUtils.removeIgnoreCase("queued", "ue") = "qd"
6005     * StringUtils.removeIgnoreCase("queued", "zz") = "queued"
6006     * StringUtils.removeIgnoreCase("quEUed", "UE") = "qd"
6007     * StringUtils.removeIgnoreCase("queued", "zZ") = "queued"
6008     * </pre>
6009     *
6010     * @param str
6011     *            the source String to search, may be null
6012     * @param remove
6013     *            the String to search for (case-insensitive) and remove, may be
6014     *            null
6015     * @return the substring with the string removed if found, {@code null} if
6016     *         null String input
6017     * @since 3.5
6018     */
6019    public static String removeIgnoreCase(final String str, final String remove) {
6020        return replaceIgnoreCase(str, remove, EMPTY, -1);
6021    }
6022
6023    /**
6024     * Removes each substring of the source String that matches the given regular expression using the DOTALL option.
6025     *
6026     * This call is a {@code null} safe equivalent to:
6027     * <ul>
6028     * <li>{@code source.replaceAll(&quot;(?s)&quot; + regex, StringUtils.EMPTY)}</li>
6029     * <li>{@code Pattern.compile(regex, Pattern.DOTALL).matcher(source).replaceAll(StringUtils.EMPTY)}</li>
6030     * </ul>
6031     *
6032     * <p>A {@code null} reference passed to this method is a no-op.</p>
6033     *
6034     * <pre>
6035     * StringUtils.removePattern(null, *)       = null
6036     * StringUtils.removePattern("any", (String) null)   = "any"
6037     * StringUtils.removePattern("A&lt;__&gt;\n&lt;__&gt;B", "&lt;.*&gt;")  = "AB"
6038     * StringUtils.removePattern("ABCabc123", "[a-z]")    = "ABC123"
6039     * </pre>
6040     *
6041     * @param source
6042     *            the source string
6043     * @param regex
6044     *            the regular expression to which this string is to be matched
6045     * @return The resulting {@link String}
6046     * @see #replacePattern(String, String, String)
6047     * @see String#replaceAll(String, String)
6048     * @see Pattern#DOTALL
6049     * @since 3.2
6050     * @since 3.5 Changed {@code null} reference passed to this method is a no-op.
6051     *
6052     * @deprecated Moved to RegExUtils.
6053     */
6054    @Deprecated
6055    public static String removePattern(final String source, final String regex) {
6056        return RegExUtils.removePattern(source, regex);
6057    }
6058
6059    /**
6060     * Removes a char only if it is at the beginning of a source string,
6061     * otherwise returns the source string.
6062     *
6063     * <p>A {@code null} source string will return {@code null}.
6064     * An empty ("") source string will return the empty string.
6065     * A {@code null} search char will return the source string.</p>
6066     *
6067     * <pre>
6068     * StringUtils.removeStart(null, *)      = null
6069     * StringUtils.removeStart("", *)        = ""
6070     * StringUtils.removeStart(*, null)      = *
6071     * StringUtils.removeStart("/path", '/') = "path"
6072     * StringUtils.removeStart("path", '/')  = "path"
6073     * StringUtils.removeStart("path", 0)    = "path"
6074     * </pre>
6075     *
6076     * @param str  the source String to search, may be null.
6077     * @param remove  the char to search for and remove.
6078     * @return the substring with the char removed if found,
6079     *  {@code null} if null String input.
6080     * @since 3.13.0
6081     */
6082    public static String removeStart(final String str, final char remove) {
6083        if (isEmpty(str)) {
6084            return str;
6085        }
6086        return str.charAt(0) == remove ? str.substring(1) : str;
6087    }
6088
6089    /**
6090     * Removes a substring only if it is at the beginning of a source string,
6091     * otherwise returns the source string.
6092     *
6093     * <p>A {@code null} source string will return {@code null}.
6094     * An empty ("") source string will return the empty string.
6095     * A {@code null} search string will return the source string.</p>
6096     *
6097     * <pre>
6098     * StringUtils.removeStart(null, *)      = null
6099     * StringUtils.removeStart("", *)        = ""
6100     * StringUtils.removeStart(*, null)      = *
6101     * StringUtils.removeStart("www.domain.com", "www.")   = "domain.com"
6102     * StringUtils.removeStart("domain.com", "www.")       = "domain.com"
6103     * StringUtils.removeStart("www.domain.com", "domain") = "www.domain.com"
6104     * StringUtils.removeStart("abc", "")    = "abc"
6105     * </pre>
6106     *
6107     * @param str  the source String to search, may be null
6108     * @param remove  the String to search for and remove, may be null
6109     * @return the substring with the string removed if found,
6110     *  {@code null} if null String input
6111     * @since 2.1
6112     */
6113    public static String removeStart(final String str, final String remove) {
6114        if (isEmpty(str) || isEmpty(remove)) {
6115            return str;
6116        }
6117        if (str.startsWith(remove)) {
6118            return str.substring(remove.length());
6119        }
6120        return str;
6121    }

6123    /**
6124     * Case insensitive removal of a substring if it is at the beginning of a source string,
6125     * otherwise returns the source string.
6126     *
6127     * <p>A {@code null} source string will return {@code null}.
6128     * An empty ("") source string will return the empty string.
6129     * A {@code null} search string will return the source string.</p>
6130     *
6131     * <pre>
6132     * StringUtils.removeStartIgnoreCase(null, *)      = null
6133     * StringUtils.removeStartIgnoreCase("", *)        = ""
6134     * StringUtils.removeStartIgnoreCase(*, null)      = *
6135     * StringUtils.removeStartIgnoreCase("www.domain.com", "www.")   = "domain.com"
6136     * StringUtils.removeStartIgnoreCase("www.domain.com", "WWW.")   = "domain.com"
6137     * StringUtils.removeStartIgnoreCase("domain.com", "www.")       = "domain.com"
6138     * StringUtils.removeStartIgnoreCase("www.domain.com", "domain") = "www.domain.com"
6139     * StringUtils.removeStartIgnoreCase("abc", "")    = "abc"
6140     * </pre>
6141     *
6142     * @param str  the source String to search, may be null
6143     * @param remove  the String to search for (case-insensitive) and remove, may be null
6144     * @return the substring with the string removed if found,
6145     *  {@code null} if null String input
6146     * @since 2.4
6147     */
6148    public static String removeStartIgnoreCase(final String str, final String remove) {
6149        if (str != null && startsWithIgnoreCase(str, remove)) {
6150            return str.substring(length(remove));
6151        }
6152        return str;
6153    }
6154
6155    /**
6156     * Returns padding using the specified delimiter repeated
6157     * to a given length.
6158     *
6159     * <pre>
6160     * StringUtils.repeat('e', 0)  = ""
6161     * StringUtils.repeat('e', 3)  = "eee"
6162     * StringUtils.repeat('e', -2) = ""
6163     * </pre>
6164     *
6165     * <p>Note: this method does not support padding with
6166     * <a href="https://www.unicode.org/glossary/#supplementary_character">Unicode Supplementary Characters</a>
6167     * as they require a pair of {@code char}s to be represented.
6168     * If you are needing to support full I18N of your applications
6169     * consider using {@link #repeat(String, int)} instead.
6170     * </p>
6171     *
6172     * @param ch  character to repeat
6173     * @param repeat  number of times to repeat char, negative treated as zero
6174     * @return String with repeated character
6175     * @see #repeat(String, int)
6176     */
6177    public static String repeat(final char ch, final int repeat) {
6178        if (repeat <= 0) {
6179            return EMPTY;
6180        }
6181        final char[] buf = new char[repeat];
6182        Arrays.fill(buf, ch);
6183        return new String(buf);
6184    }
6185
6186    /**
6187     * Repeat a String {@code repeat} times to form a
6188     * new String.
6189     *
6190     * <pre>
6191     * StringUtils.repeat(null, 2) = null
6192     * StringUtils.repeat("", 0)   = ""
6193     * StringUtils.repeat("", 2)   = ""
6194     * StringUtils.repeat("a", 3)  = "aaa"
6195     * StringUtils.repeat("ab", 2) = "abab"
6196     * StringUtils.repeat("a", -2) = ""
6197     * </pre>
6198     *
6199     * @param str  the String to repeat, may be null
6200     * @param repeat  number of times to repeat str, negative treated as zero
6201     * @return a new String consisting of the original String repeated,
6202     *  {@code null} if null String input
6203     */
6204    public static String repeat(final String str, final int repeat) {
6205        // Performance tuned for 2.0 (JDK1.4)
6206        if (str == null) {
6207            return null;
6208        }
6209        if (repeat <= 0) {
6210            return EMPTY;
6211        }
6212        final int inputLength = str.length();
6213        if (repeat == 1 || inputLength == 0) {
6214            return str;
6215        }
6216        if (inputLength == 1 && repeat <= PAD_LIMIT) {
6217            return repeat(str.charAt(0), repeat);
6218        }
6219
6220        final int outputLength = inputLength * repeat;
6221        switch (inputLength) {
6222            case 1 :
6223                return repeat(str.charAt(0), repeat);
6224            case 2 :
6225                final char ch0 = str.charAt(0);
6226                final char ch1 = str.charAt(1);
6227                final char[] output2 = new char[outputLength];
6228                for (int i = repeat * 2 - 2; i >= 0; i--, i--) {
6229                    output2[i] = ch0;
6230                    output2[i + 1] = ch1;
6231                }
6232                return new String(output2);
6233            default :
6234                final StringBuilder buf = new StringBuilder(outputLength);
6235                for (int i = 0; i < repeat; i++) {
6236                    buf.append(str);
6237                }
6238                return buf.toString();
6239        }
6240    }
6241
6242    /**
6243     * Repeat a String {@code repeat} times to form a
6244     * new String, with a String separator injected each time.
6245     *
6246     * <pre>
6247     * StringUtils.repeat(null, null, 2) = null
6248     * StringUtils.repeat(null, "x", 2)  = null
6249     * StringUtils.repeat("", null, 0)   = ""
6250     * StringUtils.repeat("", "", 2)     = ""
6251     * StringUtils.repeat("", "x", 3)    = "xx"
6252     * StringUtils.repeat("?", ", ", 3)  = "?, ?, ?"
6253     * </pre>
6254     *
6255     * @param str        the String to repeat, may be null
6256     * @param separator  the String to inject, may be null
6257     * @param repeat     number of times to repeat str, negative treated as zero
6258     * @return a new String consisting of the original String repeated,
6259     *  {@code null} if null String input
6260     * @since 2.5
6261     */
6262    public static String repeat(final String str, final String separator, final int repeat) {
6263        if (str == null || separator == null) {
6264            return repeat(str, repeat);
6265        }
6266        // given that repeat(String, int) is quite optimized, better to rely on it than try and splice this into it
6267        final String result = repeat(str + separator, repeat);
6268        return removeEnd(result, separator);
6269    }

6271    /**
6272     * Replaces all occurrences of a String within another String.
6273     *
6274     * <p>A {@code null} reference passed to this method is a no-op.</p>
6275     *
6276     * <pre>
6277     * StringUtils.replace(null, *, *)        = null
6278     * StringUtils.replace("", *, *)          = ""
6279     * StringUtils.replace("any", null, *)    = "any"
6280     * StringUtils.replace("any", *, null)    = "any"
6281     * StringUtils.replace("any", "", *)      = "any"
6282     * StringUtils.replace("aba", "a", null)  = "aba"
6283     * StringUtils.replace("aba", "a", "")    = "b"
6284     * StringUtils.replace("aba", "a", "z")   = "zbz"
6285     * </pre>
6286     *
6287     * @see #replace(String text, String searchString, String replacement, int max)
6288     * @param text  text to search and replace in, may be null
6289     * @param searchString  the String to search for, may be null
6290     * @param replacement  the String to replace it with, may be null
6291     * @return the text with any replacements processed,
6292     *  {@code null} if null String input
6293     */
6294    public static String replace(final String text, final String searchString, final String replacement) {
6295        return replace(text, searchString, replacement, -1);
6296    }
6297
6298    /**
6299     * Replaces a String with another String inside a larger String,
6300     * for the first {@code max} values of the search String.
6301     *
6302     * <p>A {@code null} reference passed to this method is a no-op.</p>
6303     *
6304     * <pre>
6305     * StringUtils.replace(null, *, *, *)         = null
6306     * StringUtils.replace("", *, *, *)           = ""
6307     * StringUtils.replace("any", null, *, *)     = "any"
6308     * StringUtils.replace("any", *, null, *)     = "any"
6309     * StringUtils.replace("any", "", *, *)       = "any"
6310     * StringUtils.replace("any", *, *, 0)        = "any"
6311     * StringUtils.replace("abaa", "a", null, -1) = "abaa"
6312     * StringUtils.replace("abaa", "a", "", -1)   = "b"
6313     * StringUtils.replace("abaa", "a", "z", 0)   = "abaa"
6314     * StringUtils.replace("abaa", "a", "z", 1)   = "zbaa"
6315     * StringUtils.replace("abaa", "a", "z", 2)   = "zbza"
6316     * StringUtils.replace("abaa", "a", "z", -1)  = "zbzz"
6317     * </pre>
6318     *
6319     * @param text  text to search and replace in, may be null
6320     * @param searchString  the String to search for, may be null
6321     * @param replacement  the String to replace it with, may be null
6322     * @param max  maximum number of values to replace, or {@code -1} if no maximum
6323     * @return the text with any replacements processed,
6324     *  {@code null} if null String input
6325     */
6326    public static String replace(final String text, final String searchString, final String replacement, final int max) {
6327        return replace(text, searchString, replacement, max, false);
6328    }
6329
6330    /**
6331     * Replaces a String with another String inside a larger String,
6332     * for the first {@code max} values of the search String,
6333     * case-sensitively/insensitively based on {@code ignoreCase} value.
6334     *
6335     * <p>A {@code null} reference passed to this method is a no-op.</p>
6336     *
6337     * <pre>
6338     * StringUtils.replace(null, *, *, *, false)         = null
6339     * StringUtils.replace("", *, *, *, false)           = ""
6340     * StringUtils.replace("any", null, *, *, false)     = "any"
6341     * StringUtils.replace("any", *, null, *, false)     = "any"
6342     * StringUtils.replace("any", "", *, *, false)       = "any"
6343     * StringUtils.replace("any", *, *, 0, false)        = "any"
6344     * StringUtils.replace("abaa", "a", null, -1, false) = "abaa"
6345     * StringUtils.replace("abaa", "a", "", -1, false)   = "b"
6346     * StringUtils.replace("abaa", "a", "z", 0, false)   = "abaa"
6347     * StringUtils.replace("abaa", "A", "z", 1, false)   = "abaa"
6348     * StringUtils.replace("abaa", "A", "z", 1, true)   = "zbaa"
6349     * StringUtils.replace("abAa", "a", "z", 2, true)   = "zbza"
6350     * StringUtils.replace("abAa", "a", "z", -1, true)  = "zbzz"
6351     * </pre>
6352     *
6353     * @param text  text to search and replace in, may be null
6354     * @param searchString  the String to search for (case-insensitive), may be null
6355     * @param replacement  the String to replace it with, may be null
6356     * @param max  maximum number of values to replace, or {@code -1} if no maximum
6357     * @param ignoreCase if true replace is case-insensitive, otherwise case-sensitive
6358     * @return the text with any replacements processed,
6359     *  {@code null} if null String input
6360     */
6361     private static String replace(final String text, String searchString, final String replacement, int max, final boolean ignoreCase) {
6362         if (isEmpty(text) || isEmpty(searchString) || replacement == null || max == 0) {
6363             return text;
6364         }
6365         if (ignoreCase) {
6366             searchString = searchString.toLowerCase();
6367         }
6368         int start = 0;
6369         int end = ignoreCase ? indexOfIgnoreCase(text, searchString, start) : indexOf(text, searchString, start);
6370         if (end == INDEX_NOT_FOUND) {
6371             return text;
6372         }
6373         final int replLength = searchString.length();
6374         int increase = Math.max(replacement.length() - replLength, 0);
6375         increase *= max < 0 ? 16 : Math.min(max, 64);
6376         final StringBuilder buf = new StringBuilder(text.length() + increase);
6377         while (end != INDEX_NOT_FOUND) {
6378             buf.append(text, start, end).append(replacement);
6379             start = end + replLength;
6380             if (--max == 0) {
6381                 break;
6382             }
6383             end = ignoreCase ? indexOfIgnoreCase(text, searchString, start) : indexOf(text, searchString, start);
6384         }
6385         buf.append(text, start, text.length());
6386         return buf.toString();
6387     }
6388
6389    /**
6390     * Replaces each substring of the text String that matches the given regular expression
6391     * with the given replacement.
6392     *
6393     * This method is a {@code null} safe equivalent to:
6394     * <ul>
6395     *  <li>{@code text.replaceAll(regex, replacement)}</li>
6396     *  <li>{@code Pattern.compile(regex).matcher(text).replaceAll(replacement)}</li>
6397     * </ul>
6398     *
6399     * <p>A {@code null} reference passed to this method is a no-op.</p>
6400     *
6401     * <p>Unlike in the {@link #replacePattern(String, String, String)} method, the {@link Pattern#DOTALL} option
6402     * is NOT automatically added.
6403     * To use the DOTALL option prepend {@code "(?s)"} to the regex.
6404     * DOTALL is also known as single-line mode in Perl.</p>
6405     *
6406     * <pre>
6407     * StringUtils.replaceAll(null, *, *)       = null
6408     * StringUtils.replaceAll("any", (String) null, *)   = "any"
6409     * StringUtils.replaceAll("any", *, null)   = "any"
6410     * StringUtils.replaceAll("", "", "zzz")    = "zzz"
6411     * StringUtils.replaceAll("", ".*", "zzz")  = "zzz"
6412     * StringUtils.replaceAll("", ".+", "zzz")  = ""
6413     * StringUtils.replaceAll("abc", "", "ZZ")  = "ZZaZZbZZcZZ"
6414     * StringUtils.replaceAll("&lt;__&gt;\n&lt;__&gt;", "&lt;.*&gt;", "z")      = "z\nz"
6415     * StringUtils.replaceAll("&lt;__&gt;\n&lt;__&gt;", "(?s)&lt;.*&gt;", "z")  = "z"
6416     * StringUtils.replaceAll("ABCabc123", "[a-z]", "_")       = "ABC___123"
6417     * StringUtils.replaceAll("ABCabc123", "[^A-Z0-9]+", "_")  = "ABC_123"
6418     * StringUtils.replaceAll("ABCabc123", "[^A-Z0-9]+", "")   = "ABC123"
6419     * StringUtils.replaceAll("Lorem ipsum  dolor   sit", "( +)([a-z]+)", "_$2")  = "Lorem_ipsum_dolor_sit"
6420     * </pre>
6421     *
6422     * @param text  text to search and replace in, may be null
6423     * @param regex  the regular expression to which this string is to be matched
6424     * @param replacement  the string to be substituted for each match
6425     * @return  the text with any replacements processed,
6426     *              {@code null} if null String input
6427     *
6428     * @throws  java.util.regex.PatternSyntaxException
6429     *              if the regular expression's syntax is invalid
6430     *
6431     * @see #replacePattern(String, String, String)
6432     * @see String#replaceAll(String, String)
6433     * @see java.util.regex.Pattern
6434     * @see java.util.regex.Pattern#DOTALL
6435     * @since 3.5
6436     *
6437     * @deprecated Moved to RegExUtils.
6438     */
6439    @Deprecated
6440    public static String replaceAll(final String text, final String regex, final String replacement) {
6441        return RegExUtils.replaceAll(text, regex, replacement);
6442    }
6443
6444    /**
6445     * Replaces all occurrences of a character in a String with another.
6446     * This is a null-safe version of {@link String#replace(char, char)}.
6447     *
6448     * <p>A {@code null} string input returns {@code null}.
6449     * An empty ("") string input returns an empty string.</p>
6450     *
6451     * <pre>
6452     * StringUtils.replaceChars(null, *, *)        = null
6453     * StringUtils.replaceChars("", *, *)          = ""
6454     * StringUtils.replaceChars("abcba", 'b', 'y') = "aycya"
6455     * StringUtils.replaceChars("abcba", 'z', 'y') = "abcba"
6456     * </pre>
6457     *
6458     * @param str  String to replace characters in, may be null
6459     * @param searchChar  the character to search for, may be null
6460     * @param replaceChar  the character to replace, may be null
6461     * @return modified String, {@code null} if null string input
6462     * @since 2.0
6463     */
6464    public static String replaceChars(final String str, final char searchChar, final char replaceChar) {
6465        if (str == null) {
6466            return null;
6467        }
6468        return str.replace(searchChar, replaceChar);
6469    }
6470
6471    /**
6472     * Replaces multiple characters in a String in one go.
6473     * This method can also be used to delete characters.
6474     *
6475     * <p>For example:<br>
6476     * {@code replaceChars(&quot;hello&quot;, &quot;ho&quot;, &quot;jy&quot;) = jelly}.</p>
6477     *
6478     * <p>A {@code null} string input returns {@code null}.
6479     * An empty ("") string input returns an empty string.
6480     * A null or empty set of search characters returns the input string.</p>
6481     *
6482     * <p>The length of the search characters should normally equal the length
6483     * of the replace characters.
6484     * If the search characters is longer, then the extra search characters
6485     * are deleted.
6486     * If the search characters is shorter, then the extra replace characters
6487     * are ignored.</p>
6488     *
6489     * <pre>
6490     * StringUtils.replaceChars(null, *, *)           = null
6491     * StringUtils.replaceChars("", *, *)             = ""
6492     * StringUtils.replaceChars("abc", null, *)       = "abc"
6493     * StringUtils.replaceChars("abc", "", *)         = "abc"
6494     * StringUtils.replaceChars("abc", "b", null)     = "ac"
6495     * StringUtils.replaceChars("abc", "b", "")       = "ac"
6496     * StringUtils.replaceChars("abcba", "bc", "yz")  = "ayzya"
6497     * StringUtils.replaceChars("abcba", "bc", "y")   = "ayya"
6498     * StringUtils.replaceChars("abcba", "bc", "yzx") = "ayzya"
6499     * </pre>
6500     *
6501     * @param str  String to replace characters in, may be null
6502     * @param searchChars  a set of characters to search for, may be null
6503     * @param replaceChars  a set of characters to replace, may be null
6504     * @return modified String, {@code null} if null string input
6505     * @since 2.0
6506     */
6507    public static String replaceChars(final String str, final String searchChars, String replaceChars) {
6508        if (isEmpty(str) || isEmpty(searchChars)) {
6509            return str;
6510        }
6511        if (replaceChars == null) {
6512            replaceChars = EMPTY;
6513        }
6514        boolean modified = false;
6515        final int replaceCharsLength = replaceChars.length();
6516        final int strLength = str.length();
6517        final StringBuilder buf = new StringBuilder(strLength);
6518        for (int i = 0; i < strLength; i++) {
6519            final char ch = str.charAt(i);
6520            final int index = searchChars.indexOf(ch);
6521            if (index >= 0) {
6522                modified = true;
6523                if (index < replaceCharsLength) {
6524                    buf.append(replaceChars.charAt(index));
6525                }
6526            } else {
6527                buf.append(ch);
6528            }
6529        }
6530        if (modified) {
6531            return buf.toString();
6532        }
6533        return str;
6534    }
6535
6536    /**
6537     * Replaces all occurrences of Strings within another String.
6538     *
6539     * <p>
6540     * A {@code null} reference passed to this method is a no-op, or if
6541     * any "search string" or "string to replace" is null, that replace will be
6542     * ignored. This will not repeat. For repeating replaces, call the
6543     * overloaded method.
6544     * </p>
6545     *
6546     * <pre>
6547     *  StringUtils.replaceEach(null, *, *)        = null
6548     *  StringUtils.replaceEach("", *, *)          = ""
6549     *  StringUtils.replaceEach("aba", null, null) = "aba"
6550     *  StringUtils.replaceEach("aba", new String[0], null) = "aba"
6551     *  StringUtils.replaceEach("aba", null, new String[0]) = "aba"
6552     *  StringUtils.replaceEach("aba", new String[]{"a"}, null)  = "aba"
6553     *  StringUtils.replaceEach("aba", new String[]{"a"}, new String[]{""})  = "b"
6554     *  StringUtils.replaceEach("aba", new String[]{null}, new String[]{"a"})  = "aba"
6555     *  StringUtils.replaceEach("abcde", new String[]{"ab", "d"}, new String[]{"w", "t"})  = "wcte"
6556     *  (example of how it does not repeat)
6557     *  StringUtils.replaceEach("abcde", new String[]{"ab", "d"}, new String[]{"d", "t"})  = "dcte"
6558     * </pre>
6559     *
6560     * @param text
6561     *            text to search and replace in, no-op if null
6562     * @param searchList
6563     *            the Strings to search for, no-op if null
6564     * @param replacementList
6565     *            the Strings to replace them with, no-op if null
6566     * @return the text with any replacements processed, {@code null} if
6567     *         null String input
6568     * @throws IllegalArgumentException
6569     *             if the lengths of the arrays are not the same (null is ok,
6570     *             and/or size 0)
6571     * @since 2.4
6572     */
6573    public static String replaceEach(final String text, final String[] searchList, final String[] replacementList) {
6574        return replaceEach(text, searchList, replacementList, false, 0);
6575    }
6576
6577    /**
6578     * Replace all occurrences of Strings within another String.
6579     * This is a private recursive helper method for {@link #replaceEachRepeatedly(String, String[], String[])} and
6580     * {@link #replaceEach(String, String[], String[])}
6581     *
6582     * <p>
6583     * A {@code null} reference passed to this method is a no-op, or if
6584     * any "search string" or "string to replace" is null, that replace will be
6585     * ignored.
6586     * </p>
6587     *
6588     * <pre>
6589     *  StringUtils.replaceEach(null, *, *, *, *) = null
6590     *  StringUtils.replaceEach("", *, *, *, *) = ""
6591     *  StringUtils.replaceEach("aba", null, null, *, *) = "aba"
6592     *  StringUtils.replaceEach("aba", new String[0], null, *, *) = "aba"
6593     *  StringUtils.replaceEach("aba", null, new String[0], *, *) = "aba"
6594     *  StringUtils.replaceEach("aba", new String[]{"a"}, null, *, *) = "aba"
6595     *  StringUtils.replaceEach("aba", new String[]{"a"}, new String[]{""}, *, >=0) = "b"
6596     *  StringUtils.replaceEach("aba", new String[]{null}, new String[]{"a"}, *, >=0) = "aba"
6597     *  StringUtils.replaceEach("abcde", new String[]{"ab", "d"}, new String[]{"w", "t"}, *, >=0) = "wcte"
6598     *  (example of how it repeats)
6599     *  StringUtils.replaceEach("abcde", new String[]{"ab", "d"}, new String[]{"d", "t"}, false, >=0) = "dcte"
6600     *  StringUtils.replaceEach("abcde", new String[]{"ab", "d"}, new String[]{"d", "t"}, true, >=2) = "tcte"
6601     *  StringUtils.replaceEach("abcde", new String[]{"ab", "d"}, new String[]{"d", "ab"}, *, *) = IllegalStateException
6602     * </pre>
6603     *
6604     * @param text
6605     *            text to search and replace in, no-op if null
6606     * @param searchList
6607     *            the Strings to search for, no-op if null
6608     * @param replacementList
6609     *            the Strings to replace them with, no-op if null
6610     * @param repeat if true, then replace repeatedly
6611     *       until there are no more possible replacements or timeToLive < 0
6612     * @param timeToLive
6613     *            if less than 0 then there is a circular reference and endless
6614     *            loop
6615     * @return the text with any replacements processed, {@code null} if
6616     *         null String input
6617     * @throws IllegalStateException
6618     *             if the search is repeating and there is an endless loop due
6619     *             to outputs of one being inputs to another
6620     * @throws IllegalArgumentException
6621     *             if the lengths of the arrays are not the same (null is ok,
6622     *             and/or size 0)
6623     * @since 2.4
6624     */
6625    private static String replaceEach(
6626            final String text, final String[] searchList, final String[] replacementList, final boolean repeat, final int timeToLive) {
6627
6628        // mchyzer Performance note: This creates very few new objects (one major goal)
6629        // let me know if there are performance requests, we can create a harness to measure
6630
6631        // if recursing, this shouldn't be less than 0
6632        if (timeToLive < 0) {
6633            final Set<String> searchSet = new HashSet<>(Arrays.asList(searchList));
6634            final Set<String> replacementSet = new HashSet<>(Arrays.asList(replacementList));
6635            searchSet.retainAll(replacementSet);
6636            if (!searchSet.isEmpty()) {
6637                throw new IllegalStateException("Aborting to protect against StackOverflowError - " +
6638                        "output of one loop is the input of another");
6639            }
6640        }
6641
6642        if (isEmpty(text) || ArrayUtils.isEmpty(searchList) || ArrayUtils.isEmpty(replacementList) || ArrayUtils.isNotEmpty(searchList) && timeToLive == -1) {
6643            return text;
6644        }
6645
6646        final int searchLength = searchList.length;
6647        final int replacementLength = replacementList.length;
6648
6649        // make sure lengths are ok, these need to be equal
6650        if (searchLength != replacementLength) {
6651            throw new IllegalArgumentException("Search and Replace array lengths don't match: "
6652                + searchLength
6653                + " vs "
6654                + replacementLength);
6655        }
6656
6657        // keep track of which still have matches
6658        final boolean[] noMoreMatchesForReplIndex = new boolean[searchLength];
6659
6660        // index on index that the match was found
6661        int textIndex = -1;
6662        int replaceIndex = -1;
6663        int tempIndex;
6664
6665        // index of replace array that will replace the search string found
6666        // NOTE: logic duplicated below START
6667        for (int i = 0; i < searchLength; i++) {
6668            if (noMoreMatchesForReplIndex[i] || isEmpty(searchList[i]) || replacementList[i] == null) {
6669                continue;
6670            }
6671            tempIndex = text.indexOf(searchList[i]);
6672
6673            // see if we need to keep searching for this
6674            if (tempIndex == -1) {
6675                noMoreMatchesForReplIndex[i] = true;
6676            } else if (textIndex == -1 || tempIndex < textIndex) {
6677                textIndex = tempIndex;
6678                replaceIndex = i;
6679            }
6680        }
6681        // NOTE: logic mostly below END
6682
6683        // no search strings found, we are done
6684        if (textIndex == -1) {
6685            return text;
6686        }
6687
6688        int start = 0;
6689
6690        // get a good guess on the size of the result buffer so it doesn't have to double if it goes over a bit
6691        int increase = 0;
6692
6693        // count the replacement text elements that are larger than their corresponding text being replaced
6694        for (int i = 0; i < searchList.length; i++) {
6695            if (searchList[i] == null || replacementList[i] == null) {
6696                continue;
6697            }
6698            final int greater = replacementList[i].length() - searchList[i].length();
6699            if (greater > 0) {
6700                increase += 3 * greater; // assume 3 matches
6701            }
6702        }
6703        // have upper-bound at 20% increase, then let Java take over
6704        increase = Math.min(increase, text.length() / 5);
6705
6706        final StringBuilder buf = new StringBuilder(text.length() + increase);
6707
6708        while (textIndex != -1) {
6709
6710            for (int i = start; i < textIndex; i++) {
6711                buf.append(text.charAt(i));
6712            }
6713            buf.append(replacementList[replaceIndex]);
6714
6715            start = textIndex + searchList[replaceIndex].length();
6716
6717            textIndex = -1;
6718            replaceIndex = -1;
6719            // find the next earliest match
6720            // NOTE: logic mostly duplicated above START
6721            for (int i = 0; i < searchLength; i++) {
6722                if (noMoreMatchesForReplIndex[i] || isEmpty(searchList[i]) || replacementList[i] == null) {
6723                    continue;
6724                }
6725                tempIndex = text.indexOf(searchList[i], start);
6726
6727                // see if we need to keep searching for this
6728                if (tempIndex == -1) {
6729                    noMoreMatchesForReplIndex[i] = true;
6730                } else if (textIndex == -1 || tempIndex < textIndex) {
6731                    textIndex = tempIndex;
6732                    replaceIndex = i;
6733                }
6734            }
6735            // NOTE: logic duplicated above END
6736
6737        }
6738        final int textLength = text.length();
6739        for (int i = start; i < textLength; i++) {
6740            buf.append(text.charAt(i));
6741        }
6742        final String result = buf.toString();
6743        if (!repeat) {
6744            return result;
6745        }
6746
6747        return replaceEach(result, searchList, replacementList, repeat, timeToLive - 1);
6748    }
6749
6750    /**
6751     * Replaces all occurrences of Strings within another String.
6752     *
6753     * <p>
6754     * A {@code null} reference passed to this method is a no-op, or if
6755     * any "search string" or "string to replace" is null, that replace will be
6756     * ignored.
6757     * </p>
6758     *
6759     * <pre>
6760     *  StringUtils.replaceEachRepeatedly(null, *, *) = null
6761     *  StringUtils.replaceEachRepeatedly("", *, *) = ""
6762     *  StringUtils.replaceEachRepeatedly("aba", null, null) = "aba"
6763     *  StringUtils.replaceEachRepeatedly("aba", new String[0], null) = "aba"
6764     *  StringUtils.replaceEachRepeatedly("aba", null, new String[0]) = "aba"
6765     *  StringUtils.replaceEachRepeatedly("aba", new String[]{"a"}, null) = "aba"
6766     *  StringUtils.replaceEachRepeatedly("aba", new String[]{"a"}, new String[]{""}) = "b"
6767     *  StringUtils.replaceEachRepeatedly("aba", new String[]{null}, new String[]{"a"}) = "aba"
6768     *  StringUtils.replaceEachRepeatedly("abcde", new String[]{"ab", "d"}, new String[]{"w", "t"}) = "wcte"
6769     *  (example of how it repeats)
6770     *  StringUtils.replaceEachRepeatedly("abcde", new String[]{"ab", "d"}, new String[]{"d", "t"}) = "tcte"
6771     *  StringUtils.replaceEachRepeatedly("abcde", new String[]{"ab", "d"}, new String[]{"d", "ab"}) = IllegalStateException
6772     * </pre>
6773     *
6774     * @param text
6775     *            text to search and replace in, no-op if null
6776     * @param searchList
6777     *            the Strings to search for, no-op if null
6778     * @param replacementList
6779     *            the Strings to replace them with, no-op if null
6780     * @return the text with any replacements processed, {@code null} if
6781     *         null String input
6782     * @throws IllegalStateException
6783     *             if the search is repeating and there is an endless loop due
6784     *             to outputs of one being inputs to another
6785     * @throws IllegalArgumentException
6786     *             if the lengths of the arrays are not the same (null is ok,
6787     *             and/or size 0)
6788     * @since 2.4
6789     */
6790    public static String replaceEachRepeatedly(final String text, final String[] searchList, final String[] replacementList) {
6791        return replaceEach(text, searchList, replacementList, true, ArrayUtils.getLength(searchList));
6792    }

6794    /**
6795     * Replaces the first substring of the text string that matches the given regular expression
6796     * with the given replacement.
6797     *
6798     * This method is a {@code null} safe equivalent to:
6799     * <ul>
6800     *  <li>{@code text.replaceFirst(regex, replacement)}</li>
6801     *  <li>{@code Pattern.compile(regex).matcher(text).replaceFirst(replacement)}</li>
6802     * </ul>
6803     *
6804     * <p>A {@code null} reference passed to this method is a no-op.</p>
6805     *
6806     * <p>The {@link Pattern#DOTALL} option is NOT automatically added.
6807     * To use the DOTALL option prepend {@code "(?s)"} to the regex.
6808     * DOTALL is also known as single-line mode in Perl.</p>
6809     *
6810     * <pre>
6811     * StringUtils.replaceFirst(null, *, *)       = null
6812     * StringUtils.replaceFirst("any", (String) null, *)   = "any"
6813     * StringUtils.replaceFirst("any", *, null)   = "any"
6814     * StringUtils.replaceFirst("", "", "zzz")    = "zzz"
6815     * StringUtils.replaceFirst("", ".*", "zzz")  = "zzz"
6816     * StringUtils.replaceFirst("", ".+", "zzz")  = ""
6817     * StringUtils.replaceFirst("abc", "", "ZZ")  = "ZZabc"
6818     * StringUtils.replaceFirst("&lt;__&gt;\n&lt;__&gt;", "&lt;.*&gt;", "z")      = "z\n&lt;__&gt;"
6819     * StringUtils.replaceFirst("&lt;__&gt;\n&lt;__&gt;", "(?s)&lt;.*&gt;", "z")  = "z"
6820     * StringUtils.replaceFirst("ABCabc123", "[a-z]", "_")          = "ABC_bc123"
6821     * StringUtils.replaceFirst("ABCabc123abc", "[^A-Z0-9]+", "_")  = "ABC_123abc"
6822     * StringUtils.replaceFirst("ABCabc123abc", "[^A-Z0-9]+", "")   = "ABC123abc"
6823     * StringUtils.replaceFirst("Lorem ipsum  dolor   sit", "( +)([a-z]+)", "_$2")  = "Lorem_ipsum  dolor   sit"
6824     * </pre>
6825     *
6826     * @param text  text to search and replace in, may be null
6827     * @param regex  the regular expression to which this string is to be matched
6828     * @param replacement  the string to be substituted for the first match
6829     * @return  the text with the first replacement processed,
6830     *              {@code null} if null String input
6831     *
6832     * @throws  java.util.regex.PatternSyntaxException
6833     *              if the regular expression's syntax is invalid
6834     *
6835     * @see String#replaceFirst(String, String)
6836     * @see java.util.regex.Pattern
6837     * @see java.util.regex.Pattern#DOTALL
6838     * @since 3.5
6839     *
6840     * @deprecated Moved to RegExUtils.
6841     */
6842    @Deprecated
6843    public static String replaceFirst(final String text, final String regex, final String replacement) {
6844        return RegExUtils.replaceFirst(text, regex, replacement);
6845    }

6847    /**
6848     * Case insensitively replaces all occurrences of a String within another String.
6849     *
6850     * <p>A {@code null} reference passed to this method is a no-op.</p>
6851     *
6852     * <pre>
6853     * StringUtils.replaceIgnoreCase(null, *, *)        = null
6854     * StringUtils.replaceIgnoreCase("", *, *)          = ""
6855     * StringUtils.replaceIgnoreCase("any", null, *)    = "any"
6856     * StringUtils.replaceIgnoreCase("any", *, null)    = "any"
6857     * StringUtils.replaceIgnoreCase("any", "", *)      = "any"
6858     * StringUtils.replaceIgnoreCase("aba", "a", null)  = "aba"
6859     * StringUtils.replaceIgnoreCase("abA", "A", "")    = "b"
6860     * StringUtils.replaceIgnoreCase("aba", "A", "z")   = "zbz"
6861     * </pre>
6862     *
6863     * @see #replaceIgnoreCase(String text, String searchString, String replacement, int max)
6864     * @param text  text to search and replace in, may be null
6865     * @param searchString  the String to search for (case-insensitive), may be null
6866     * @param replacement  the String to replace it with, may be null
6867     * @return the text with any replacements processed,
6868     *  {@code null} if null String input
6869     * @since 3.5
6870     */
6871     public static String replaceIgnoreCase(final String text, final String searchString, final String replacement) {
6872         return replaceIgnoreCase(text, searchString, replacement, -1);
6873     }

6875    /**
6876     * Case insensitively replaces a String with another String inside a larger String,
6877     * for the first {@code max} values of the search String.
6878     *
6879     * <p>A {@code null} reference passed to this method is a no-op.</p>
6880     *
6881     * <pre>
6882     * StringUtils.replaceIgnoreCase(null, *, *, *)         = null
6883     * StringUtils.replaceIgnoreCase("", *, *, *)           = ""
6884     * StringUtils.replaceIgnoreCase("any", null, *, *)     = "any"
6885     * StringUtils.replaceIgnoreCase("any", *, null, *)     = "any"
6886     * StringUtils.replaceIgnoreCase("any", "", *, *)       = "any"
6887     * StringUtils.replaceIgnoreCase("any", *, *, 0)        = "any"
6888     * StringUtils.replaceIgnoreCase("abaa", "a", null, -1) = "abaa"
6889     * StringUtils.replaceIgnoreCase("abaa", "a", "", -1)   = "b"
6890     * StringUtils.replaceIgnoreCase("abaa", "a", "z", 0)   = "abaa"
6891     * StringUtils.replaceIgnoreCase("abaa", "A", "z", 1)   = "zbaa"
6892     * StringUtils.replaceIgnoreCase("abAa", "a", "z", 2)   = "zbza"
6893     * StringUtils.replaceIgnoreCase("abAa", "a", "z", -1)  = "zbzz"
6894     * </pre>
6895     *
6896     * @param text  text to search and replace in, may be null
6897     * @param searchString  the String to search for (case-insensitive), may be null
6898     * @param replacement  the String to replace it with, may be null
6899     * @param max  maximum number of values to replace, or {@code -1} if no maximum
6900     * @return the text with any replacements processed,
6901     *  {@code null} if null String input
6902     * @since 3.5
6903     */
6904    public static String replaceIgnoreCase(final String text, final String searchString, final String replacement, final int max) {
6905        return replace(text, searchString, replacement, max, true);
6906    }

6915     * StringUtils.replaceOnce("", *, *)          = ""
6916     * StringUtils.replaceOnce("any", null, *)    = "any"
6917     * StringUtils.replaceOnce("any", *, null)    = "any"
6918     * StringUtils.replaceOnce("any", "", *)      = "any"
6919     * StringUtils.replaceOnce("aba", "a", null)  = "aba"
6920     * StringUtils.replaceOnce("aba", "a", "")    = "ba"
6921     * StringUtils.replaceOnce("aba", "a", "z")   = "zba"
6922     * </pre>
6923     *

6925     * @param text  text to search and replace in, may be null
6926     * @param searchString  the String to search for, may be null

6931    public static String replaceOnce(final String text, final String searchString, final String replacement) {

6936     * Case insensitively replaces a String with another String inside a larger String, once.
6937     *
6938     * <p>A {@code null} reference passed to this method is a no-op.</p>
6939     *
6940     * <pre>
6941     * StringUtils.replaceOnceIgnoreCase(null, *, *)        = null
6942     * StringUtils.replaceOnceIgnoreCase("", *, *)          = ""
6943     * StringUtils.replaceOnceIgnoreCase("any", null, *)    = "any"
6944     * StringUtils.replaceOnceIgnoreCase("any", *, null)    = "any"
6945     * StringUtils.replaceOnceIgnoreCase("any", "", *)      = "any"
6946     * StringUtils.replaceOnceIgnoreCase("aba", "a", null)  = "aba"
6947     * StringUtils.replaceOnceIgnoreCase("aba", "a", "")    = "ba"
6948     * StringUtils.replaceOnceIgnoreCase("aba", "a", "z")   = "zba"
6949     * StringUtils.replaceOnceIgnoreCase("FoOFoofoo", "foo", "") = "Foofoo"
6950     * </pre>
6951     *
6952     * @see #replaceIgnoreCase(String text, String searchString, String replacement, int max)
6953     * @param text  text to search and replace in, may be null
6954     * @param searchString  the String to search for (case-insensitive), may be null
6955     * @param replacement  the String to replace with, may be null
6956     * @return the text with any replacements processed,
6957     *  {@code null} if null String input
6958     * @since 3.5
6959     */
6960    public static String replaceOnceIgnoreCase(final String text, final String searchString, final String replacement) {
6961        return replaceIgnoreCase(text, searchString, replacement, 1);
6962    }

6964    /**
6965     * Replaces each substring of the source String that matches the given regular expression with the given
6966     * replacement using the {@link Pattern#DOTALL} option. DOTALL is also known as single-line mode in Perl.
6967     *
6968     * This call is a {@code null} safe equivalent to:
6969     * <ul>
6970     * <li>{@code source.replaceAll(&quot;(?s)&quot; + regex, replacement)}</li>
6971     * <li>{@code Pattern.compile(regex, Pattern.DOTALL).matcher(source).replaceAll(replacement)}</li>
6972     * </ul>
6973     *
6974     * <p>A {@code null} reference passed to this method is a no-op.</p>
6975     *
6976     * <pre>
6977     * StringUtils.replacePattern(null, *, *)       = null
6978     * StringUtils.replacePattern("any", (String) null, *)   = "any"
6979     * StringUtils.replacePattern("any", *, null)   = "any"
6980     * StringUtils.replacePattern("", "", "zzz")    = "zzz"
6981     * StringUtils.replacePattern("", ".*", "zzz")  = "zzz"
6982     * StringUtils.replacePattern("", ".+", "zzz")  = ""
6983     * StringUtils.replacePattern("&lt;__&gt;\n&lt;__&gt;", "&lt;.*&gt;", "z")       = "z"
6984     * StringUtils.replacePattern("ABCabc123", "[a-z]", "_")       = "ABC___123"
6985     * StringUtils.replacePattern("ABCabc123", "[^A-Z0-9]+", "_")  = "ABC_123"
6986     * StringUtils.replacePattern("ABCabc123", "[^A-Z0-9]+", "")   = "ABC123"
6987     * StringUtils.replacePattern("Lorem ipsum  dolor   sit", "( +)([a-z]+)", "_$2")  = "Lorem_ipsum_dolor_sit"
6988     * </pre>
6989     *
6990     * @param source
6991     *            the source string
6992     * @param regex
6993     *            the regular expression to which this string is to be matched
6994     * @param replacement
6995     *            the string to be substituted for each match
6996     * @return The resulting {@link String}
6997     * @see #replaceAll(String, String, String)
6998     * @see String#replaceAll(String, String)
6999     * @see Pattern#DOTALL
7000     * @since 3.2
7001     * @since 3.5 Changed {@code null} reference passed to this method is a no-op.
7002     *
7003     * @deprecated Moved to RegExUtils.
7004     */
7005    @Deprecated
7006    public static String replacePattern(final String source, final String regex, final String replacement) {
7007        return RegExUtils.replacePattern(source, regex, replacement);
7008    }

7010    /**
7011     * Reverses a String as per {@link StringBuilder#reverse()}.
7012     *
7013     * <p>A {@code null} String returns {@code null}.</p>
7014     *
7015     * <pre>
7016     * StringUtils.reverse(null)  = null
7017     * StringUtils.reverse("")    = ""
7018     * StringUtils.reverse("bat") = "tab"
7019     * </pre>
7020     *
7021     * @param str  the String to reverse, may be null
7022     * @return the reversed String, {@code null} if null String input
7023     */
7024    public static String reverse(final String str) {
7025        if (str == null) {
7026            return null;
7027        }
7028        return new StringBuilder(str).reverse().toString();
7029    }
7030
7031    /**
7032     * Reverses a String that is delimited by a specific character.
7033     *
7034     * <p>The Strings between the delimiters are not reversed.
7035     * Thus java.lang.String becomes String.lang.java (if the delimiter
7036     * is {@code '.'}).</p>
7037     *
7038     * <pre>
7039     * StringUtils.reverseDelimited(null, *)      = null
7040     * StringUtils.reverseDelimited("", *)        = ""
7041     * StringUtils.reverseDelimited("a.b.c", 'x') = "a.b.c"
7042     * StringUtils.reverseDelimited("a.b.c", ".") = "c.b.a"
7043     * </pre>
7044     *
7045     * @param str  the String to reverse, may be null
7046     * @param separatorChar  the separator character to use
7047     * @return the reversed String, {@code null} if null String input
7048     * @since 2.0
7049     */
7050    public static String reverseDelimited(final String str, final char separatorChar) {
7051        if (str == null) {
7052            return null;
7053        }
7054        // could implement manually, but simple way is to reuse other,
7055        // probably slower, methods.
7056        final String[] strs = split(str, separatorChar);
7057        ArrayUtils.reverse(strs);
7058        return join(strs, separatorChar);
7059    }
7060
7061    /**
7062     * Gets the rightmost {@code len} characters of a String.
7063     *
7064     * <p>If {@code len} characters are not available, or the String
7065     * is {@code null}, the String will be returned without an
7066     * an exception. An empty String is returned if len is negative.</p>
7067     *
7068     * <pre>
7069     * StringUtils.right(null, *)    = null
7070     * StringUtils.right(*, -ve)     = ""
7071     * StringUtils.right("", *)      = ""
7072     * StringUtils.right("abc", 0)   = ""
7073     * StringUtils.right("abc", 2)   = "bc"
7074     * StringUtils.right("abc", 4)   = "abc"
7075     * </pre>
7076     *
7077     * @param str  the String to get the rightmost characters from, may be null
7078     * @param len  the length of the required String
7079     * @return the rightmost characters, {@code null} if null String input
7080     */
7081    public static String right(final String str, final int len) {
7082        if (str == null) {
7083            return null;
7084        }
7085        if (len < 0) {
7086            return EMPTY;
7087        }
7088        if (str.length() <= len) {
7089            return str;
7090        }
7091        return str.substring(str.length() - len);
7092    }
7093
7094    /**
7095     * Right pad a String with spaces (' ').
7096     *
7097     * <p>The String is padded to the size of {@code size}.</p>
7098     *
7099     * <pre>
7100     * StringUtils.rightPad(null, *)   = null
7101     * StringUtils.rightPad("", 3)     = "   "
7102     * StringUtils.rightPad("bat", 3)  = "bat"
7103     * StringUtils.rightPad("bat", 5)  = "bat  "
7104     * StringUtils.rightPad("bat", 1)  = "bat"
7105     * StringUtils.rightPad("bat", -1) = "bat"
7106     * </pre>
7107     *
7108     * @param str  the String to pad out, may be null
7109     * @param size  the size to pad to
7110     * @return right padded String or original String if no padding is necessary,
7111     *  {@code null} if null String input
7112     */
7113    public static String rightPad(final String str, final int size) {
7114        return rightPad(str, size, ' ');
7115    }
7116
7117    /**
7118     * Right pad a String with a specified character.
7119     *
7120     * <p>The String is padded to the size of {@code size}.</p>
7121     *
7122     * <pre>
7123     * StringUtils.rightPad(null, *, *)     = null
7124     * StringUtils.rightPad("", 3, 'z')     = "zzz"
7125     * StringUtils.rightPad("bat", 3, 'z')  = "bat"
7126     * StringUtils.rightPad("bat", 5, 'z')  = "batzz"
7127     * StringUtils.rightPad("bat", 1, 'z')  = "bat"
7128     * StringUtils.rightPad("bat", -1, 'z') = "bat"
7129     * </pre>
7130     *
7131     * @param str  the String to pad out, may be null
7132     * @param size  the size to pad to
7133     * @param padChar  the character to pad with
7134     * @return right padded String or original String if no padding is necessary,
7135     *  {@code null} if null String input
7136     * @since 2.0
7137     */
7138    public static String rightPad(final String str, final int size, final char padChar) {
7139        if (str == null) {
7140            return null;
7141        }
7142        final int pads = size - str.length();
7143        if (pads <= 0) {
7144            return str; // returns original String when possible
7145        }
7146        if (pads > PAD_LIMIT) {
7147            return rightPad(str, size, String.valueOf(padChar));
7148        }
7149        return str.concat(repeat(padChar, pads));
7150    }
7151
7152    /**
7153     * Right pad a String with a specified String.
7154     *
7155     * <p>The String is padded to the size of {@code size}.</p>
7156     *
7157     * <pre>
7158     * StringUtils.rightPad(null, *, *)      = null
7159     * StringUtils.rightPad("", 3, "z")      = "zzz"
7160     * StringUtils.rightPad("bat", 3, "yz")  = "bat"
7161     * StringUtils.rightPad("bat", 5, "yz")  = "batyz"
7162     * StringUtils.rightPad("bat", 8, "yz")  = "batyzyzy"
7163     * StringUtils.rightPad("bat", 1, "yz")  = "bat"
7164     * StringUtils.rightPad("bat", -1, "yz") = "bat"
7165     * StringUtils.rightPad("bat", 5, null)  = "bat  "
7166     * StringUtils.rightPad("bat", 5, "")    = "bat  "
7167     * </pre>
7168     *
7169     * @param str  the String to pad out, may be null
7170     * @param size  the size to pad to
7171     * @param padStr  the String to pad with, null or empty treated as single space
7172     * @return right padded String or original String if no padding is necessary,
7173     *  {@code null} if null String input
7174     */
7175    public static String rightPad(final String str, final int size, String padStr) {
7176        if (str == null) {
7177            return null;
7178        }
7179        if (isEmpty(padStr)) {
7180            padStr = SPACE;
7181        }
7182        final int padLen = padStr.length();
7183        final int strLen = str.length();
7184        final int pads = size - strLen;
7185        if (pads <= 0) {
7186            return str; // returns original String when possible
7187        }
7188        if (padLen == 1 && pads <= PAD_LIMIT) {
7189            return rightPad(str, size, padStr.charAt(0));
7190        }
7191
7192        if (pads == padLen) {
7193            return str.concat(padStr);
7194        }
7195        if (pads < padLen) {
7196            return str.concat(padStr.substring(0, pads));
7197        }
7198        final char[] padding = new char[pads];
7199        final char[] padChars = padStr.toCharArray();
7200        for (int i = 0; i < pads; i++) {
7201            padding[i] = padChars[i % padLen];
7202        }
7203        return str.concat(new String(padding));
7204    }
7205
7206    /**
7207     * Rotate (circular shift) a String of {@code shift} characters.
7208     * <ul>
7209     *  <li>If {@code shift > 0}, right circular shift (ex : ABCDEF =&gt; FABCDE)</li>
7210     *  <li>If {@code shift < 0}, left circular shift (ex : ABCDEF =&gt; BCDEFA)</li>
7211     * </ul>
7212     *
7213     * <pre>
7214     * StringUtils.rotate(null, *)        = null
7215     * StringUtils.rotate("", *)          = ""
7216     * StringUtils.rotate("abcdefg", 0)   = "abcdefg"
7217     * StringUtils.rotate("abcdefg", 2)   = "fgabcde"
7218     * StringUtils.rotate("abcdefg", -2)  = "cdefgab"
7219     * StringUtils.rotate("abcdefg", 7)   = "abcdefg"
7220     * StringUtils.rotate("abcdefg", -7)  = "abcdefg"
7221     * StringUtils.rotate("abcdefg", 9)   = "fgabcde"
7222     * StringUtils.rotate("abcdefg", -9)  = "cdefgab"
7223     * </pre>
7224     *
7225     * @param str  the String to rotate, may be null
7226     * @param shift  number of time to shift (positive : right shift, negative : left shift)
7227     * @return the rotated String,
7228     *          or the original String if {@code shift == 0},
7229     *          or {@code null} if null String input
7230     * @since 3.5
7231     */
7232    public static String rotate(final String str, final int shift) {
7233        if (str == null) {
7234            return null;
7235        }
7236
7237        final int strLen = str.length();
7238        if (shift == 0 || strLen == 0 || shift % strLen == 0) {
7239            return str;
7240        }
7241
7242        final StringBuilder builder = new StringBuilder(strLen);
7243        final int offset = - (shift % strLen);
7244        builder.append(substring(str, offset));
7245        builder.append(substring(str, 0, offset));
7246        return builder.toString();
7247    }

7249    /**
7250     * Splits the provided text into an array, using whitespace as the
7251     * separator.
7252     * Whitespace is defined by {@link Character#isWhitespace(char)}.
7253     *
7254     * <p>The separator is not included in the returned String array.
7255     * Adjacent separators are treated as one separator.
7256     * For more control over the split use the StrTokenizer class.</p>
7257     *
7258     * <p>A {@code null} input String returns {@code null}.</p>
7259     *
7260     * <pre>
7261     * StringUtils.split(null)       = null
7262     * StringUtils.split("")         = []
7263     * StringUtils.split("abc def")  = ["abc", "def"]
7264     * StringUtils.split("abc  def") = ["abc", "def"]
7265     * StringUtils.split(" abc ")    = ["abc"]
7266     * </pre>
7267     *
7268     * @param str  the String to parse, may be null
7269     * @return an array of parsed Strings, {@code null} if null String input
7270     */
7271    public static String[] split(final String str) {
7272        return split(str, null, -1);
7273    }

7332    /**

7335     *
7336     * <p>The separator is not included in the returned String array.

7344     * returned strings (including separator characters).</p>

7350     * StringUtils.split("ab   cd ef", null, 0) = ["ab", "cd", "ef"]

7353     * </pre>

7355     * @param str  the String to parse, may be null
7356     * @param separatorChars  the characters used as the delimiters,
7357     *  {@code null} splits on whitespace

7359     *  array. A zero or negative value implies no limit
7360     * @return an array of parsed Strings, {@code null} if null String input
7361     */
7362    public static String[] split(final String str, final String separatorChars, final int max) {
7363        return splitWorker(str, separatorChars, max, false);
7364    }

7366    /**
7367     * Splits a String by Character type as returned by
7368     * {@code java.lang.Character.getType(char)}. Groups of contiguous
7369     * characters of the same type are returned as complete tokens.
7370     * <pre>
7371     * StringUtils.splitByCharacterType(null)         = null
7372     * StringUtils.splitByCharacterType("")           = []
7373     * StringUtils.splitByCharacterType("ab de fg")   = ["ab", " ", "de", " ", "fg"]
7374     * StringUtils.splitByCharacterType("ab   de fg") = ["ab", "   ", "de", " ", "fg"]
7375     * StringUtils.splitByCharacterType("ab:cd:ef")   = ["ab", ":", "cd", ":", "ef"]
7376     * StringUtils.splitByCharacterType("number5")    = ["number", "5"]
7377     * StringUtils.splitByCharacterType("fooBar")     = ["foo", "B", "ar"]
7378     * StringUtils.splitByCharacterType("foo200Bar")  = ["foo", "200", "B", "ar"]
7379     * StringUtils.splitByCharacterType("ASFRules")   = ["ASFR", "ules"]
7380     * </pre>
7381     * @param str the String to split, may be {@code null}
7382     * @return an array of parsed Strings, {@code null} if null String input
7383     * @since 2.4
7384     */
7385    public static String[] splitByCharacterType(final String str) {
7386        return splitByCharacterType(str, false);
7387    }
7388
7389    /**
7390     * <p>Splits a String by Character type as returned by
7391     * {@code java.lang.Character.getType(char)}. Groups of contiguous
7392     * characters of the same type are returned as complete tokens, with the
7393     * following exception: if {@code camelCase} is {@code true},
7394     * the character of type {@code Character.UPPERCASE_LETTER}, if any,
7395     * immediately preceding a token of type {@code Character.LOWERCASE_LETTER}
7396     * will belong to the following token rather than to the preceding, if any,
7397     * {@code Character.UPPERCASE_LETTER} token.
7398     * @param str the String to split, may be {@code null}
7399     * @param camelCase whether to use so-called "camel-case" for letter types
7400     * @return an array of parsed Strings, {@code null} if null String input
7401     * @since 2.4
7402     */
7403    private static String[] splitByCharacterType(final String str, final boolean camelCase) {
7404        if (str == null) {
7405            return null;
7406        }
7407        if (str.isEmpty()) {
7408            return ArrayUtils.EMPTY_STRING_ARRAY;
7409        }
7410        final char[] c = str.toCharArray();
7411        final List<String> list = new ArrayList<>();
7412        int tokenStart = 0;
7413        int currentType = Character.getType(c[tokenStart]);
7414        for (int pos = tokenStart + 1; pos < c.length; pos++) {
7415            final int type = Character.getType(c[pos]);
7416            if (type == currentType) {
7417                continue;
7418            }
7419            if (camelCase && type == Character.LOWERCASE_LETTER && currentType == Character.UPPERCASE_LETTER) {
7420                final int newTokenStart = pos - 1;
7421                if (newTokenStart != tokenStart) {
7422                    list.add(new String(c, tokenStart, newTokenStart - tokenStart));
7423                    tokenStart = newTokenStart;
7424                }
7425            } else {
7426                list.add(new String(c, tokenStart, pos - tokenStart));
7427                tokenStart = pos;
7428            }
7429            currentType = type;
7430        }
7431        list.add(new String(c, tokenStart, c.length - tokenStart));
7432        return list.toArray(ArrayUtils.EMPTY_STRING_ARRAY);
7433    }
7434
7435    /**
7436     * <p>Splits a String by Character type as returned by
7437     * {@code java.lang.Character.getType(char)}. Groups of contiguous
7438     * characters of the same type are returned as complete tokens, with the
7439     * following exception: the character of type
7440     * {@code Character.UPPERCASE_LETTER}, if any, immediately
7441     * preceding a token of type {@code Character.LOWERCASE_LETTER}
7442     * will belong to the following token rather than to the preceding, if any,
7443     * {@code Character.UPPERCASE_LETTER} token.
7444     * <pre>
7445     * StringUtils.splitByCharacterTypeCamelCase(null)         = null
7446     * StringUtils.splitByCharacterTypeCamelCase("")           = []
7447     * StringUtils.splitByCharacterTypeCamelCase("ab de fg")   = ["ab", " ", "de", " ", "fg"]
7448     * StringUtils.splitByCharacterTypeCamelCase("ab   de fg") = ["ab", "   ", "de", " ", "fg"]
7449     * StringUtils.splitByCharacterTypeCamelCase("ab:cd:ef")   = ["ab", ":", "cd", ":", "ef"]
7450     * StringUtils.splitByCharacterTypeCamelCase("number5")    = ["number", "5"]
7451     * StringUtils.splitByCharacterTypeCamelCase("fooBar")     = ["foo", "Bar"]
7452     * StringUtils.splitByCharacterTypeCamelCase("foo200Bar")  = ["foo", "200", "Bar"]
7453     * StringUtils.splitByCharacterTypeCamelCase("ASFRules")   = ["ASF", "Rules"]
7454     * </pre>
7455     * @param str the String to split, may be {@code null}
7456     * @return an array of parsed Strings, {@code null} if null String input
7457     * @since 2.4
7458     */
7459    public static String[] splitByCharacterTypeCamelCase(final String str) {
7460        return splitByCharacterType(str, true);
7461    }

7476     * StringUtils.splitByWholeSeparator("ab   de fg", null)    = ["ab", "de", "fg"]

7550    /**
7551     * Splits the provided text into an array, separator string specified.
7552     * Returns a maximum of {@code max} substrings.
7553     *
7554     * <p>The separator is not included in the returned String array.
7555     * Adjacent separators are treated as separators for empty tokens.
7556     * For more control over the split use the StrTokenizer class.</p>
7557     *
7558     * <p>A {@code null} input String returns {@code null}.
7559     * A {@code null} separator splits on whitespace.</p>
7560     *
7561     * <pre>
7562     * StringUtils.splitByWholeSeparatorPreserveAllTokens(null, *, *)               = null
7563     * StringUtils.splitByWholeSeparatorPreserveAllTokens("", *, *)                 = []
7564     * StringUtils.splitByWholeSeparatorPreserveAllTokens("ab de fg", null, 0)      = ["ab", "de", "fg"]
7565     * StringUtils.splitByWholeSeparatorPreserveAllTokens("ab   de fg", null, 0)    = ["ab", "", "", "de", "fg"]
7566     * StringUtils.splitByWholeSeparatorPreserveAllTokens("ab:cd:ef", ":", 2)       = ["ab", "cd:ef"]
7567     * StringUtils.splitByWholeSeparatorPreserveAllTokens("ab-!-cd-!-ef", "-!-", 5) = ["ab", "cd", "ef"]
7568     * StringUtils.splitByWholeSeparatorPreserveAllTokens("ab-!-cd-!-ef", "-!-", 2) = ["ab", "cd-!-ef"]
7569     * </pre>
7570     *
7571     * @param str  the String to parse, may be null
7572     * @param separator  String containing the String to be used as a delimiter,
7573     *  {@code null} splits on whitespace
7574     * @param max  the maximum number of elements to include in the returned
7575     *  array. A zero or negative value implies no limit.
7576     * @return an array of parsed Strings, {@code null} if null String was input
7577     * @since 2.4
7578     */
7579    public static String[] splitByWholeSeparatorPreserveAllTokens(final String str, final String separator, final int max) {
7580        return splitByWholeSeparatorWorker(str, separator, max, true);
7581    }
7582
7583    /**
7584     * Performs the logic for the {@code splitByWholeSeparatorPreserveAllTokens} methods.
7585     *
7586     * @param str  the String to parse, may be {@code null}
7587     * @param separator  String containing the String to be used as a delimiter,
7588     *  {@code null} splits on whitespace
7589     * @param max  the maximum number of elements to include in the returned
7590     *  array. A zero or negative value implies no limit.
7591     * @param preserveAllTokens if {@code true}, adjacent separators are
7592     * treated as empty token separators; if {@code false}, adjacent
7593     * separators are treated as one separator.
7594     * @return an array of parsed Strings, {@code null} if null String input
7595     * @since 2.4
7596     */
7597    private static String[] splitByWholeSeparatorWorker(
7598            final String str, final String separator, final int max, final boolean preserveAllTokens) {
7599        if (str == null) {
7600            return null;
7601        }
7602
7603        final int len = str.length();
7604
7605        if (len == 0) {
7606            return ArrayUtils.EMPTY_STRING_ARRAY;
7607        }
7608
7609        if (separator == null || EMPTY.equals(separator)) {
7610            // Split on whitespace.
7611            return splitWorker(str, null, max, preserveAllTokens);
7612        }
7613
7614        final int separatorLength = separator.length();
7615
7616        final ArrayList<String> substrings = new ArrayList<>();
7617        int numberOfSubstrings = 0;
7618        int beg = 0;
7619        int end = 0;
7620        while (end < len) {
7621            end = str.indexOf(separator, beg);
7622
7623            if (end > -1) {
7624                if (end > beg) {
7625                    numberOfSubstrings += 1;
7626
7627                    if (numberOfSubstrings == max) {
7628                        end = len;
7629                        substrings.add(str.substring(beg));
7630                    } else {
7631                        // The following is OK, because String.substring( beg, end ) excludes
7632                        // the character at the position 'end'.
7633                        substrings.add(str.substring(beg, end));
7634
7635                        // Set the starting point for the next search.
7636                        // The following is equivalent to beg = end + (separatorLength - 1) + 1,
7637                        // which is the right calculation:
7638                        beg = end + separatorLength;
7639                    }
7640                } else {
7641                    // We found a consecutive occurrence of the separator, so skip it.
7642                    if (preserveAllTokens) {
7643                        numberOfSubstrings += 1;
7644                        if (numberOfSubstrings == max) {
7645                            end = len;
7646                            substrings.add(str.substring(beg));
7647                        } else {
7648                            substrings.add(EMPTY);
7649                        }
7650                    }
7651                    beg = end + separatorLength;
7652                }
7653            } else {
7654                // String.substring( beg ) goes from 'beg' to the end of the String.
7655                substrings.add(str.substring(beg));
7656                end = len;
7657            }
7658        }
7659
7660        return substrings.toArray(ArrayUtils.EMPTY_STRING_ARRAY);
7661    }
7662
7663    /**
7664     * Splits the provided text into an array, using whitespace as the
7665     * separator, preserving all tokens, including empty tokens created by
7666     * adjacent separators. This is an alternative to using StringTokenizer.
7667     * Whitespace is defined by {@link Character#isWhitespace(char)}.
7668     *
7669     * <p>The separator is not included in the returned String array.
7670     * Adjacent separators are treated as separators for empty tokens.
7671     * For more control over the split use the StrTokenizer class.</p>
7672     *
7673     * <p>A {@code null} input String returns {@code null}.</p>
7674     *
7675     * <pre>
7676     * StringUtils.splitPreserveAllTokens(null)       = null
7677     * StringUtils.splitPreserveAllTokens("")         = []
7678     * StringUtils.splitPreserveAllTokens("abc def")  = ["abc", "def"]
7679     * StringUtils.splitPreserveAllTokens("abc  def") = ["abc", "", "def"]
7680     * StringUtils.splitPreserveAllTokens(" abc ")    = ["", "abc", ""]
7681     * </pre>
7682     *
7683     * @param str  the String to parse, may be {@code null}
7684     * @return an array of parsed Strings, {@code null} if null String input
7685     * @since 2.1
7686     */
7687    public static String[] splitPreserveAllTokens(final String str) {
7688        return splitWorker(str, null, -1, true);
7689    }
7690
7691    /**
7692     * Splits the provided text into an array, separator specified,
7693     * preserving all tokens, including empty tokens created by adjacent
7694     * separators. This is an alternative to using StringTokenizer.
7695     *
7696     * <p>The separator is not included in the returned String array.
7697     * Adjacent separators are treated as separators for empty tokens.
7698     * For more control over the split use the StrTokenizer class.</p>
7699     *
7700     * <p>A {@code null} input String returns {@code null}.</p>
7701     *
7702     * <pre>
7703     * StringUtils.splitPreserveAllTokens(null, *)         = null
7704     * StringUtils.splitPreserveAllTokens("", *)           = []
7705     * StringUtils.splitPreserveAllTokens("a.b.c", '.')    = ["a", "b", "c"]
7706     * StringUtils.splitPreserveAllTokens("a..b.c", '.')   = ["a", "", "b", "c"]
7707     * StringUtils.splitPreserveAllTokens("a:b:c", '.')    = ["a:b:c"]
7708     * StringUtils.splitPreserveAllTokens("a\tb\nc", null) = ["a", "b", "c"]
7709     * StringUtils.splitPreserveAllTokens("a b c", ' ')    = ["a", "b", "c"]
7710     * StringUtils.splitPreserveAllTokens("a b c ", ' ')   = ["a", "b", "c", ""]
7711     * StringUtils.splitPreserveAllTokens("a b c  ", ' ')   = ["a", "b", "c", "", ""]
7712     * StringUtils.splitPreserveAllTokens(" a b c", ' ')   = ["", a", "b", "c"]
7713     * StringUtils.splitPreserveAllTokens("  a b c", ' ')  = ["", "", a", "b", "c"]
7714     * StringUtils.splitPreserveAllTokens(" a b c ", ' ')  = ["", a", "b", "c", ""]
7715     * </pre>
7716     *
7717     * @param str  the String to parse, may be {@code null}
7718     * @param separatorChar  the character used as the delimiter,
7719     *  {@code null} splits on whitespace
7720     * @return an array of parsed Strings, {@code null} if null String input
7721     * @since 2.1
7722     */
7723    public static String[] splitPreserveAllTokens(final String str, final char separatorChar) {
7724        return splitWorker(str, separatorChar, true);
7725    }

7727    /**
7728     * Splits the provided text into an array, separators specified,
7729     * preserving all tokens, including empty tokens created by adjacent
7730     * separators. This is an alternative to using StringTokenizer.
7731     *
7732     * <p>The separator is not included in the returned String array.
7733     * Adjacent separators are treated as separators for empty tokens.
7734     * For more control over the split use the StrTokenizer class.</p>
7735     *
7736     * <p>A {@code null} input String returns {@code null}.
7737     * A {@code null} separatorChars splits on whitespace.</p>
7738     *
7739     * <pre>
7740     * StringUtils.splitPreserveAllTokens(null, *)           = null
7741     * StringUtils.splitPreserveAllTokens("", *)             = []
7742     * StringUtils.splitPreserveAllTokens("abc def", null)   = ["abc", "def"]
7743     * StringUtils.splitPreserveAllTokens("abc def", " ")    = ["abc", "def"]
7744     * StringUtils.splitPreserveAllTokens("abc  def", " ")   = ["abc", "", def"]
7745     * StringUtils.splitPreserveAllTokens("ab:cd:ef", ":")   = ["ab", "cd", "ef"]
7746     * StringUtils.splitPreserveAllTokens("ab:cd:ef:", ":")  = ["ab", "cd", "ef", ""]
7747     * StringUtils.splitPreserveAllTokens("ab:cd:ef::", ":") = ["ab", "cd", "ef", "", ""]
7748     * StringUtils.splitPreserveAllTokens("ab::cd:ef", ":")  = ["ab", "", cd", "ef"]
7749     * StringUtils.splitPreserveAllTokens(":cd:ef", ":")     = ["", cd", "ef"]
7750     * StringUtils.splitPreserveAllTokens("::cd:ef", ":")    = ["", "", cd", "ef"]
7751     * StringUtils.splitPreserveAllTokens(":cd:ef:", ":")    = ["", cd", "ef", ""]
7752     * </pre>
7753     *
7754     * @param str  the String to parse, may be {@code null}
7755     * @param separatorChars  the characters used as the delimiters,
7756     *  {@code null} splits on whitespace
7757     * @return an array of parsed Strings, {@code null} if null String input
7758     * @since 2.1
7759     */
7760    public static String[] splitPreserveAllTokens(final String str, final String separatorChars) {
7761        return splitWorker(str, separatorChars, -1, true);
7762    }
